<script type='text/javascript'>

var timeout = 500;
var closetimer = 500;
var ddmenuitem = 0;

// open hidden layer
function mopen(id)
{
// cancel close timer
mcancelclosetime();

// close old layer
if(ddmenuitem) ddmenuitem.style.visibility = 'hidden';

// get new layer and show it
ddmenuitem = document.getElementById(id);
ddmenuitem.style.visibility = 'visible';

}
// close showed layer
function mclose()
{
if(ddmenuitem) ddmenuitem.style.visibility = 'hidden';
}

// go close timer
function mclosetime()
{
closetimer = window.setTimeout(mclose, timeout);
}

// cancel close timer
function mcancelclosetime()
{
if(closetimer)
{
window.clearTimeout(closetimer);
closetimer = null;
}
}

// close layer when click-out
document.onclick = mclose;
</script>

<link href='https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NW8Mr1oo0Q0/Vqf3Efe18RI/AAAAAAAACCs/APSIVrEZ43U/s320/bP5BcmSRID0.jpg' rel='image_src' type='image/jpeg'/>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Sunday, January 31, 2016</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NW8Mr1oo0Q0/Vqf3Efe18RI/AAAAAAAACCs/APSIVrEZ43U/s320/bP5BcmSRID0.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='4968585480029088528' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='590342912771141220' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='590342912771141220'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
Tabletop Game Giveaways and Contests 1000 Member Prize Celebration!
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-590342912771141220' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NW8Mr1oo0Q0/Vqf3Efe18RI/AAAAAAAACCs/APSIVrEZ43U/s1600/bP5BcmSRID0.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="240" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NW8Mr1oo0Q0/Vqf3Efe18RI/AAAAAAAACCs/APSIVrEZ43U/s320/bP5BcmSRID0.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
I manage the Tabletop Game Giveaways and Contests group on Facebook: <a href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/TabletopGameGiveaways/" target="_blank">https://www.facebook.com/groups/TabletopGameGiveaways/</a>&nbsp; Nearly every day members of the group post new giveaways for tabletop games (and related items). &nbsp;It's a thriving community of people sharing information about the games they are passionate about and ways to win those games from the incredibly generous publishers, bloggers, and other members of the tabletop games community.<br />
<br />
We just hit 1000 members in the group as a little celebration I am organizing a big giveaway of a bunch of items. &nbsp;I've reached out to a number of sponsors and we have game prizes coming in! &nbsp;This celebration giveaway will run for the month of February As more prizes are donated to the giveaway I'll list them below. &nbsp;At the end of the month I'll draw names from all the entrants for all the prizes!<br />
<br />
Remember, <b>sponsors are encouraged to enter too!</b> &nbsp;They just can't win their own prizes! &nbsp;Thank you to everyone who is participating!<br />
<br />
<b><span style="color: orange; font-size: large;">Enter Below the Prize List!</span></b><br />
<br />

<b><span style="color: orange;">About the Sponsors:</span></b><br />
<ol style="text-align: left;">
<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-fX0qUFKQ1p0/U8V2uZXgYWI/AAAAAAAAAOE/Ei7X0TLFyWE/s1600/GJJG-Logo-sm.png" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://georgejaros.com/GJJGames" target="_blank">GJJ Games</a>&nbsp;is me, George Jaros! &nbsp;I review games, including Kickstarter previews. &nbsp;I also design my own games, which I'm hoping to publish someday soon. &nbsp;A few can be purchased on <a href="https://www.thegamecrafter.com/designers/gjj-games" target="_blank">The Game Crafter</a> and <a href="http://www.drivethrucards.com/browse/pub/9061/GJJ-Games" target="_blank">Drive Thru Cards</a>.</li>
<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="https://scontent.ford1-1.fna.fbcdn.net/hphotos-xfp1/v/t1.0-9/1476393_676314215747045_356252418_n.png?oh=da5d33784c49b716d05653b78307aa0e&amp;oe=5732C7B9" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://www.everythingboardgames.com/" target="_blank">Everything Board Games</a>&nbsp;provides information about board game deals, giveaways, reviews and more.</li>
<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="http://nebula.wsimg.com/8066f0770999a27c77b0088601eb9c52?AccessKeyId=DDD2BE717DFBF045DCDE&amp;disposition=0&amp;alloworigin=1" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://www.happyottergames.com/" target="_blank">Happy Otter Games</a>&nbsp;is currently having their first game, Creature College, manufactured to send out to the Kickstarter backers that brought the game to fruition. &nbsp;There are a few additional games in development that will be Kickstarted in the months ahead.</li>
<li><img border="0" src="https://www.thegamecrafter.com/tgc4/img/circle_logo.png" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://thegamecrafter.com/" target="_blank">The Game Crafter</a>&nbsp;is the world&#8217;s first web-to-print game publishing company and offers a print on demand game publishing service. TGC empowers game designers around the world by allowing them to make a board game, card game, and custom playing cards through a website.</li>
<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><a href="http://thegamecrafter.com/" target="_blank">The Game Crafter</a>&nbsp;is sponsoring two prizes! &nbsp;Thank you!</li>
<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="https://scontent.ford1-1.fna.fbcdn.net/hphotos-xta1/v/t1.0-9/12360258_1693903450847653_8656108099038914560_n.png?oh=ed4a3631706f7186ab4937338d9ed0a8&amp;oe=5745A105" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://smarterbacker.com/" target="_blank">Smarter Backer</a>&nbsp;is a community of crowdfunders where you can learn about and discuss the merits of Kickstarter campaigns. &nbsp;Smarter Backer is for all types of campaigns, but the primary focus is on tabletop games. &nbsp;Smarter Backer also features the weekly Zayas Index of the top campaigns each week as well as reviews and live video interviews.</li>
<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="http://nebula.wsimg.com/43029d1c6ece047cd8b168c8b5dbf815?AccessKeyId=3F0408BD2893B320BB33&amp;disposition=0&amp;alloworigin=1" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://www.knowchancegames.com/" target="_blank">Know Chance Games</a>&nbsp;is the publisher of the successful Kickstarter games, Stealing Mona Lisa, Cabaret, and The Treasury.</li>
<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="https://scontent.ford1-1.fna.fbcdn.net/hphotos-xfa1/t31.0-8/11001538_10152570578251090_9013984744007227878_o.jpg" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://setgame.com/" target="_blank">Set Enterprises</a>&nbsp;is the publisher of a number of award winning games, including&nbsp;SET, Quiddler, Five Crowns, and Karma.</li>
<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="https://scontent.ford1-1.fna.fbcdn.net/hphotos-xaf1/v/t1.0-9/1896736_363494270456050_1372032582_n.jpg?oh=b53f739758a8c3250afc26f7eaf49ebd&amp;oe=5733203C" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://www.geekygoodies.com/" target="_blank">Geeky Goodies</a>&nbsp;designs and creates T-shirts and other cool goodies for the board game community and geeks of all stripes and fandoms.</li>

<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="https://greygnome.files.wordpress.com/2014/03/newlogo.jpg?w=120&amp;h=120&amp;crop=1" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://greygnome.com/" target="_blank">Grey Gnome Games</a>&nbsp;is the publisher of a number of games, including Dig Down Dwarf, Virgin Seas, Trainmaker,&nbsp;Four Tribes, and more! &nbsp;Watch for their latest Kickstarter for Siege of Sunfall coming soon!</li>

<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="https://ksr-ugc.imgix.net/avatars/2184468/v3g_twitter.original.jpg?v=1372085588&amp;w=220&amp;h=220&amp;fit=crop&amp;auto=format&amp;q=92&amp;s=76b9e8e87ae007989214b99633961557" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://www.vision3games.com/" target="_blank">V3G</a>, aka Vision 3 Games is the publisher of&nbsp;Strife: Legacy of the Eternals and the sequel,&nbsp;<a href="https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/v3g/strife-shadows-and-steam" target="_blank">Strife: Shadows &amp; Steam</a>, which is on Kickstarter now! &nbsp;Check it out!</li>

<li><a href="http://gotgeniusgames.com/" target="_blank">Genius Games</a>&nbsp;is sponsoring three prizes! &nbsp;Thank you!</li>

<li style="margin-bottom: 25px;"><img border="0" src="https://www.thegaminggoat.com/store/templates/gamingoat/images/logo.png" style="width: 120px;" /><a href="http://www.thegaminggoat.com/" target="_blank">The Gaming Goat</a>&nbsp;is a chain of game stores in the Chicagoland area (and Henderson, NV). &nbsp;The Gaming Goat in DeKalb, IL is the FLGS of choice of GJJ Games!</li>

They also share and promote other giveaways for board game related items.</li>

The small print...</div>
<div>
<br /></div>
<div>
<i>Winners will be contacted via the email they supplied via the the contest widget. &nbsp;Winners will have 48 hours to respond before a new winner will be selected. &nbsp;Winning entries will be checked for validity, so any shares must be publicly visible. &nbsp;Shipping locations will be determined by the prize sponsors. &nbsp;Winners will be selected from all eligible entries. &nbsp;Winners will be limited to winning one prize from the pool. &nbsp;I will do my best to match up non-US winners with prizes that can be shipped internationally. &nbsp;Prize awards are the responsibility of the prize sponsor. &nbsp;I will do my best to facilitate the awarding of prizes, but ultimately it is the responsibility of the prize sponsor to deliver the agreed upon award. &nbsp;GJJ Games will only be responsible for providing prizes sponsored by GJJ Games. &nbsp;Prize sponsors are welcome to enter, but cannot win their own prize. &nbsp;GJJ Games and my immediate family are&nbsp;ineligible. &nbsp;No purchase necessary, void where prohibited, etc., etc....</i><br />

      var msgs = {'loadMore': 'Load more...', 'loading': 'Loading...', 'loaded': 'No more!', 'addComment': 'Add comment', 'reply': 'Reply', 'delete': 'Delete'};
      var config = {'blogId': '4968585480029088528', 'postId': '590342912771141220', 'feed': 'http://gjjgames.blogspot.com/feeds/590342912771141220/comments/default', 'authorName': 'George Jaros', 'authorUrl': 'https://www.blogger.com/profile/15131784120804596408', 'baseUri': 'https://www.blogger.com', 'maxThreadDepth': 2};

// <![CDATA[
      var cursor = null;
      if (items && items.length > 0) {
        cursor = parseInt(items[items.length - 1].timestamp) + 1;
      }

      var bodyFromEntry = function(entry) {
        if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
          for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.contentRemoved') {
              return '<span class="deleted-comment">' + entry.content.$t + '</span>';
            }
          }
        }
        return entry.content.$t;
      }

      var parse = function(data) {
        cursor = null;
        var comments = [];
        if (data && data.feed && data.feed.entry) {
          for (var i = 0, entry; entry = data.feed.entry[i]; i++) {
            var comment = {};
            // comment ID, parsed out of the original id format
            var id = /blog-(\d+).post-(\d+)/.exec(entry.id.$t);
            comment.id = id ? id[2] : null;
            comment.body = bodyFromEntry(entry);
            comment.timestamp = Date.parse(entry.published.$t) + '';
            if (entry.author && entry.author.constructor === Array) {
              var auth = entry.author[0];
              if (auth) {
                comment.author = {
                  name: (auth.name ? auth.name.$t : undefined),
                  profileUrl: (auth.uri ? auth.uri.$t : undefined),
                  avatarUrl: (auth.gd$image ? auth.gd$image.src : undefined)
                };
              }
            }
            if (entry.link) {
              if (entry.link[2]) {
                comment.link = comment.permalink = entry.link[2].href;
              }
              if (entry.link[3]) {
                var pid = /.*comments\/default\/(\d+)\?.*/.exec(entry.link[3].href);
                if (pid && pid[1]) {
                  comment.parentId = pid[1];
                }
              }
            }
            comment.deleteclass = 'item-control blog-admin';
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
              for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.itemClass') {
                  comment.deleteclass += ' ' + entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                } else if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.displayTime') {
                  comment.displayTime = entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                }
              }
            }
            comments.push(comment);
          }
        }
        return comments;
      };

      var paginator = function(callback) {
        if (hasMore()) {
          var url = config.feed + '?alt=json&v=2&orderby=published&reverse=false&max-results=50';
          if (cursor) {
            url += '&published-min=' + new Date(cursor).toISOString();
          }
          window.bloggercomments = function(data) {
            var parsed = parse(data);
            cursor = parsed.length < 50 ? null
                : parseInt(parsed[parsed.length - 1].timestamp) + 1
            callback(parsed);
            window.bloggercomments = null;
          }
          url += '&callback=bloggercomments';
          var script = document.createElement('script');
          script.type = 'text/javascript';
          script.src = url;
          document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
        }
      };
      var hasMore = function() {
        return !!cursor;
      };
      var getMeta = function(key, comment) {
        if ('iswriter' == key) {
          var matches = !!comment.author
              && comment.author.name == config.authorName
              && comment.author.profileUrl == config.authorUrl;
          return matches ? 'true' : '';
        } else if ('deletelink' == key) {
          return config.baseUri + '/delete-comment.g?blogID='
               + config.blogId + '&postID=' + comment.id;
        } else if ('deleteclass' == key) {
          return comment.deleteclass;
        }
        return '';
      };

      var replybox = null;
      var replyUrlParts = null;
      var replyParent = undefined;

      var onReply = function(commentId, domId) {
        if (replybox == null) {
          // lazily cache replybox, and adjust to suit this style:
          replybox = document.getElementById('comment-editor');
          if (replybox != null) {
            replybox.height = '250px';
            replybox.style.display = 'block';
            replyUrlParts = replybox.src.split('#');
          }
        }
        if (replybox && (commentId !== replyParent)) {
          replybox.src = '';
          document.getElementById(domId).insertBefore(replybox, null);
          replybox.src = replyUrlParts[0]
              + (commentId ? '&parentID=' + commentId : '')
              + '#' + replyUrlParts[1];
          replyParent = commentId;
        }
      };

      var hash = (window.location.hash || '#').substring(1);
      var startThread, targetComment;
      if (/^comment-form_/.test(hash)) {
        startThread = hash.substring('comment-form_'.length);
      } else if (/^c[0-9]+$/.test(hash)) {
        targetComment = hash.substring(1);
      }

      // Configure commenting API:
      var configJso = {
        'maxDepth': config.maxThreadDepth
      };
      var provider = {
        'id': config.postId,
        'data': items,
        'loadNext': paginator,
        'hasMore': hasMore,
        'getMeta': getMeta,
        'onReply': onReply,
        'rendered': true,
        'initComment': targetComment,
        'initReplyThread': startThread,
        'config': configJso,
        'messages': msgs
      };

      var render = function() {
        if (window.goog && window.goog.comments) {
          var holder = document.getElementById('comment-holder');
          window.goog.comments.render(holder, provider);
        }
      };

      // render now, or queue to render when library loads:
      if (window.goog && window.goog.comments) {
        render();
      } else {
        window.goog = window.goog || {};
        window.goog.comments = window.goog.comments || {};
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue = window.goog.comments.loadQueue || [];
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue.push(render);
      }
    })();
